Power BI Report Server REST API

The Power BI Report Server REST API provides programmatic access to the report server catalog. For example, basic CRUD operations can be done on folders, reports, KPIs, data sources, datasets, refresh plans, subscriptions, etc.

The REST API can also be used to provide more advanced functionality, such as:

  • Navigate the folder hierarchy
  • Discover the contents of a folder
  • Download a report definition
  • Modify default report parameters
  • Change or execute a refresh plan
  • A whole lot more

The REST API is a RESTful successor to the legacy SOAP API.

Since Power BI Report Server is a superset of SQL Server Reporting Services, the Power BI Report Server REST API is a superset of the SQL Server Reporting Services REST API.

Power BI Report Server API Additions

  • January 2019 Release
    • /PowerBIReports({Id})/DataModelRoles (GET)
    • /PowerBIReports({Id})/DataModelRoleAssignments (GET & PUT)

Happy coding!

CacheRefreshPlans

Up 
post /CacheRefreshPlans
Creates a new CacheRefreshPlan item. (addCacheRefreshPlan)

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

CacheRefreshPlan CacheRefreshPlan (required)
Body Parameter — The definition of the new CacheRefreshPlan item.

Return type

CacheRefreshPlan

Example data

{

  "Description" : "Description",

    "Value" : "Value",
    "Name" : "Name"
  } ]
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

201

The definition of the CacheRefreshPlan item that was just created. CacheRefreshPlan

400

Couldn't understand your request.

409

Conflict. Item already exists.

default

Error odata.error
Up 
delete /CacheRefreshPlans({Id})
Deletes the specified CacheRefreshPlan. (deleteCacheRefreshPlan)

Path parameters

Id (required)
Path Parameter — The GUID that uniquely identifies the CacheRefreshPlan. GUID example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef format: string

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Ok

default

Error odata.error
Up 
post /CacheRefreshPlans({Id})/Model.Execute

Path parameters

Id (required)
Path Parameter — The GUID that uniquely identifies the CacheRefreshPlan. GUID example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef format: string

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

204

The return result is empty.

default

Error odata.error

  • application/json

Return type

ODataSubscriptionHistory

    "Type" : "Scheduled",

    "Details" : "Details",

CatalogItems

post /CatalogItems
Creates a new CatalogItem. (addCatalogItem)

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

CatalogItem CatalogItem (required)
Body Parameter — The definition of the new CatalogItem.

Return type

CatalogItem

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{

Query parameters

$top (optional)
Query Parameter — Show only the first n items, see OData Paging - Top
$skip (optional)
Query Parameter — Skip the first n items, see OData Paging - Skip
$filter (optional)
Query Parameter — Filter items by property values, see OData Filtering
$count (optional)
Query Parameter — Include count of items, see OData Count
$orderBy (optional)
Query Parameter — Order items by property values, see OData Sorting
$select (optional)
Query Parameter — Select properties to be returned, see OData Select

Path Parameter — The key (GUID or path) that uniquely identifies the object. GUID example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef path example: path='/folder1/folder2/item' If the path itself contains single quote, it should be escaped - add another single quote. format: string

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Query parameters

$top (optional)
Query Parameter — Show only the first n items, see OData Paging - Top
$skip (optional)
Query Parameter — Skip the first n items, see OData Paging - Skip
$filter (optional)
Query Parameter — Filter items by property values, see OData Filtering
$count (optional)
Query Parameter — Include count of items, see OData Count
$orderBy (optional)
Query Parameter — Order items by property values, see OData Sorting
$expand (optional)
Query Parameter — Expand related entities, see OData Expand
$select (optional)
Query Parameter — Select properties to be returned, see OData Select

Return type

array[Subscription]

AllowedAction - AllowedAction Up

An object that specifies an allowed action on a CatalogItem.
Action (optional)
String The allowed action. format: string

BulkOperationsResult - BulkOperationsResult Up

Result of bulk operations like MoveItems and DeleteItems
FailedOperations (optional)
array[String]
HasErrors (optional)
Boolean format: true|false

CacheOptions - CacheOptions Up

An object that specifies options for a data cache.
ExecutionType (optional)
ItemExecutionType
Expiration (optional)
ExpirationReference

CacheRefreshPlan - CacheRefreshPlan Up

An object that specifies a plan for data cache refresh. The plan can be stored and re-used by multiple CatalogItems.
Id (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier by which this CacheRefreshPlan can be referenced in the definition of other items. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
Owner (optional)
String A string value that specifies the owner of the CacheRefreshPlan. format: string
Description (optional)
String A string value that contains descriptive text about the CacheRefreshPlan. format: string
CatalogItemPath (optional)
String A string value that contains the fully qualified URL path location of the CatalogItem that represents the CacheRefreshPlan. format: string
EventType (optional)
String A string value that specifies which EventType to use for logging. format: string
Schedule (optional)
ScheduleReference
LastRunTime (optional)
Date A date-time value that specifies the date-time of the last run of the CacheRefreshPlan. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
LastStatus (optional)
String A string value that contains the network username of the last user to modify the CacheRefreshPlan. format: string
ModifiedBy (optional)
String A string value that contains the network user name of the last user to modify the CacheRefreshPlan format: string
ModifiedDate (optional)
Date A string value that contains the date-time of the last modification to the CacheRefreshPlan. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
ParameterValues (optional)
array[ParameterValue] An array of parameter values for the CacheRefreshPlan. All parameters without a default value MUST have a value specified.

CatalogItem - CatalogItem Up

CatalogItem is an abstract type that contains the common properties of all the types of CatalogItems. Hence, it is the base type from which the other CatalogItem types are derived.
Id (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier by which this CatalogItem can be referenced in requests or by other defined objects. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
Name (optional)
String A string value that specifies the name for the CatalogItem. This name is typically displayed in the user interface. format: string
Description (optional)
String A string value that contains descriptive text about the CatalogItem. format: string
Path (optional)
String A string value that contains the full server path for the CatalogItem. Path is defined as an alternate key on the CatalogItem and can be used as the parameter by which CatalogItem can be referenced in requests or by other defined objects. format: string
Type (optional)
CatalogItemType
Hidden (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that indicates if the CatalogItem is hidden. If true, the item will generally not appear in listings of CatalogItems within the parent item. format: true|false
Size (optional)
Long An Int64 value that contains the size of the CatalogItem in bytes. format: int64
ModifiedBy (optional)
String A string value that contains the network user name of the last user to modify the CatalogItem. format: string
ModifiedDate (optional)
Date A string value that contains the date-time of the last modification to the CatalogItem. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
CreatedBy (optional)
String A string value that represents the network user name of the user who originally created the CatalogItem. format: string
CreatedDate (optional)
Date A string that contains the date-time of the creation of the CatalogItem. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
ParentFolderId (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier of the Folder CatalogItem that contains this CatalogItem. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
ContentType (optional)
String A string value that contains a SOAP MIME-type that is associated with the CatalogItem. format: string
Content (optional)
String A string value that contains binary encoding by base64url encoding rules. The value of this property is not processed by the server. In object creation the server receives and stores a value, and in object retrieval the server returns the previously stored value.
IsFavorite (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that specifies whether the CatalogItem is designated as a Favorite. format: true|false

CatalogItemType - CatalogItemType Up

An enumeration of values that specifies the type of the CatalogItem.

Comment - Comment Up

An object that specifies a comment that is attached to a CatalogItem.
Id (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier of the comment. format: uuid
ItemId (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier of the CatalogItem item to which the comment is attached. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
UserName (optional)
String A string value that represents the user who created the comment item. format: string
ThreadId (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier of the thread of the comment. A comment thread can be used to group comments that are a response to one another in one grouping. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
AttachmentPath (optional)
String A string value that specifies the server path to an attachment that is part of the comment. format: string
Text (optional)
String A string value that contains the text of the comment. format: string
CreatedDate (optional)
Date A string that contains the date-time of the creation of the comment. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
ModifiedDate (optional)
Date A string value that contains the date-time of the last modification to the comment. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z

CredentialsStoredInServer - CredentialsStoredInServer Up

This object holds credentials for connections to an external data source. The object is stored on the Report Server for later retrieval and use. Applies to DataSets, LinkedReports, and Reports. Ignored when used with PowerBIReports. For PowerBIReports, use DataSourceSubType = DataModel and DataModelDataSource.UserName and DataModelDataSource.Secret NOTE: This object represents a security risk as its properties can be seen in plain text over the HTTP protocol; HTTPS is recommended.
UserName (optional)
String A string value that contains the user name to be used to connect to an external data source. format: string
Password (optional)
String A string value that contains the password to be used to connect to an external data source. format: string
UseAsWindowsCredentials (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that indicates whether the supplied credentials should be used as Windows credentials. format: true|false
ImpersonateAuthenticatedUser (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that indicates whether the session should impersonate the user for the supplied credentials. format: true|false

CredentialsSuppliedByUser - CredentialsSuppliedByUser Up

An object that contains information about prompting a user for credentials for connections to an external data source. Applies to DataSets, LinkedReports, and Reports. Ignored when used with PowerBIReports.
DisplayText (optional)
String A string value that contains text used to prompt a user to supply credentials for connections to an external data source. format: string
UseAsWindowsCredentials (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that indicates whether credentials the user supplies in a prompt should be used as Windows credentials. format: true|false

DailyRecurrence - DailyRecurrence Up

Represents the intervals at which a scheduled report runs. Intervals are specified in days.
DaysInterval (optional)
Integer An Int32 value representing interval in days. format: int32

DataSet - Up

Id (optional)

String A string value that contains the network user name of the last user to modify the CatalogItem. format: string

example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z

String A string value that represents the network user name of the user who originally created the CatalogItem. format: string

Date A string that contains the date-time of the creation of the CatalogItem. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z

example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef

Content (optional)
String A string value that contains binary encoding by base64url encoding rules. The value of this property is not processed by the server. In object creation the server receives and stores a value, and in object retrieval the server returns the previously stored value.

An object that specifies a parameter's value as a name-value pair.

Value (optional)
String A string that contains the value for the parameter. format: string
IsValueFieldReference (optional)

Policy - Policy Up

An object that specifies a set of roles that are grouped together as a policy and can then be assigned as a group of policies to an item using the property GroupUserName.

String A string value that specifies the name of the user or group to which the policy applies. format: string
Roles (optional)
array[Role] An array of objects of type Role that specify the security roles that are included in the Policy.

PowerBIReport - Up

Id (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier by which this CatalogItem can be referenced in requests or by other defined objects. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
Name (optional)
String A string value that specifies the name for the CatalogItem. This name is typically displayed in the user interface. format: string
Description (optional)
String A string value that contains descriptive text about the CatalogItem. format: string
Path (optional)
String A string value that contains the full server path for the CatalogItem. Path is defined as an alternate key on the CatalogItem and can be used as the parameter by which CatalogItem can be referenced in requests or by other defined objects. format: string
Type (optional)
CatalogItemType
Hidden (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that indicates if the CatalogItem is hidden. If true, the item will generally not appear in listings of CatalogItems within the parent item. format: true|false
Size (optional)
Long An Int64 value that contains the size of the CatalogItem in bytes. format: int64
ModifiedBy (optional)
String A string value that contains the network user name of the last user to modify the CatalogItem. format: string
ModifiedDate (optional)
Date A string value that contains the date-time of the last modification to the CatalogItem. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
CreatedBy (optional)
String A string value that represents the network user name of the user who originally created the CatalogItem. format: string
CreatedDate (optional)
Date A string that contains the date-time of the creation of the CatalogItem. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
ParentFolderId (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier of the Folder CatalogItem that contains this CatalogItem. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
ContentType (optional)
String A string value that contains a SOAP MIME-type that is associated with the CatalogItem. format: string
Content (optional)
String A string value that contains binary encoding by base64url encoding rules. The value of this property is not processed by the server. In object creation the server receives and stores a value, and in object retrieval the server returns the previously stored value.
IsFavorite (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that specifies whether the CatalogItem is designated as a Favorite. format: true|false
HasDataSources (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that indicates whether the PowerBIReport has DataSources. format: true|false

Subscription - Subscription Up

An object that defines a subscription. A Reporting Services subscription allows a user to subscribe to a Report or Data Source and then to automatically receive an update whenever the item is updated.
Id (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that specifies the identifier by which this Subscription can be referenced in requests or in other defined objects. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
Owner (optional)
String A string value that specifies the owner of the Subscription. format: string
IsDataDriven (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that specifies whether the members of the distribution list for the subscription are computed based on data. format: true|false
Description (optional)
String A string value that contains descriptive text about the Subscription. format: string
Report (optional)
String A string value that specifies the path of the report for this Subscription. format: string
IsActive (optional)
Boolean A boolean value that specifies whether the Subscription is currently active. format: true|false
EventType (optional)
String A string specifying the type of event that triggers the Subscription. format: string
ScheduleDescription (optional)
String A string value that contains descriptive text about the schedule referenced in the Schedule property. format: string
LastRunTime (optional)
Date A string value that contains the date-time that the schedule was last run. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
LastStatus (optional)
String A string specifying the Status of the last run. format: string
ExtensionSettings (optional)
ExtensionSettings
DeliveryExtension (optional)
String An object that specifies the DeliveryExtension that will be used with this Schedule's report delivery. format: string
LocalizedDeliveryExtensionName (optional)
String Localized version of extension name when available. format: string
ModifiedBy (optional)
String A string value that contains the network user name of the last user to modify the subscription. format: string
ModifiedDate (optional)
Date A string value that contains the date-time of the last modification to the subscription. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
ParameterValues (optional)
array[ParameterValue] An array of items of type ParameterValue that specify the parameter values for the subscription.

SubscriptionHistory - SubscriptionHistory Up

An object that defines a subscription history or execution record.
Id (optional)
Integer A unique identifier by which this Subscription History record can be referenced in requests or in other defined objects. format: int32
SubscriptionID (optional)
UUID A unique UUID value that identifies the Subscription that this record is associated with. format: uuid
example: 01234567-89ab-cdef-0123-456789abcdef
Type (optional)
String A string value that specifies the type of subscription execution.
Enum:
Scheduled
OnDemand
StartTime (optional)
Date A string that contains the date-time for when the subscription execution started. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
EndTime (optional)
Date A string that contains the date-time for when the subscription execution ended. format: date-time
example: 2017-04-13T15:51:04Z
SubscriptionStatus (optional)
String A string value that represents the status of the subscription execution.
Enum:
Completed
InProgress
Failed
Message (optional)
String A string value that contains message that describes the status of the subscription execution. format: string
Details (optional)
String A JSON string value that contains the session information and error details when a subscription execution fails. format: string
